Process flow title 
Rev. 
Date of revision 
Contact email 
Graphene disks on hBN 
2.2 
19-Jul-15 
npemo@nanotech.dtu.dk 
 
Not confidential 
File name: Process_flow_grapheneDisks 
Page 2 of 3 
 
Step Heading 
Equipment 
Procedure 
Comments 
1 Preparation 
 
1.1 Sample 
wafer 
1.2 Test wafer  
 
Bring the wafer with stacks into the cleanroom  
 
Use a clean Si wafer as test wafer 
 
2 Electron beam lithography 
 
2.1 Dehydration 
bake 
Si-allowed 
hotplate 
Bake the test wafer at 200°C for 15 minutes 
Cool down hotplate 
afterwards 
2.2 PMMA resist 
coating 
Spin coater: 
Manual 
labspin 
Coat test wafer with 50 nm PMMA (not crucial) 
PMMA 996k (2wt-% PMMA) in anisole 
5 s at 500 RPM, 60 s at 4000 RPM 
 
2.3 Test wafer 
bake 
Si allowed 
hotplate 
Ramp to 120°C  
Bake wafer at 120°C for 30 min 
Ramp up to 180°C (approx. 3 min) 
Bake wafer at 180°C for 60 min 
Ramp down to room temperature (> 60 min)  
 
2.4 Measure 
thickness 
Filmtek 
Measure resist thickness on test wafer 
 
2.5 Dehydration 
bake 
Si allowed 
hotplate 
Bake the sample wafer at 200°C for 15 minutes 
Cool down hotplate 
afterwards  
2.6 PMMA resist 
coating 
Spin coater: 
Manual 
labspin 
Coat sample wafer with 50 nm PMMA (not crucial) 
PMMA 996k (2wt-% PMMA) in anisole 
5 s at 500 RPM, 60 s at 4000 RPM 
 
2.7 Sample 
wafer bake 
Si allowed 
hotplate 
Ramp to 120°C  
Bake wafer at 120°C for 30 min 
Ramp up to 180°C (approx. 3 min) 
Bake wafer at 180°C for 60 min 
Ramp down to room temperature (> 60 min) 
Measure thickness in Filmtek 
2.8 Al thermal 
coating 
Wordentec 
Deposition of 15 nm Al to avoid charge 
concentration in resist. 
OBS: Thermal evaporation 
2.9 Exposure 
JEOL E-beam 
writer 
Write graphene structures, controlled by .v30, .jdf, 
and .sdf – files 
Recommended: D = 450 um/cm2, I=0.2 nA 
 
2.10 Removal of 
Al 
Fumehood 
MF-CD26 for 60 s 
Clean with IPA 
 
2.11 PMMA 
development 
Fumehood 
MIBK:IPA (1:3) for 100 s 
Clean with IPA for 30 s 
Blow dry 
Found to overdevelop 100 
nm disks. Needs 
optimization. 
3 Etching 
 
3.1 Etch 
graphene 
III-V ICP 
10 s, 5 sccm O2, 15 sccm Ar.  
Recipe: users/lenga/graphene 
 
3.2 Strip resist 
Fumehood 
Acetone for 30 min. Clean in IPA 
Blow dry 
 
4 Characterization 
 
4.1 Optical 
inspection 
Nikon 
ECLIPSE L200 
For overview. Check for development in dark field 
mode. 
 
4.2 SEM 
inspection 
SEM-
Zeiss/Leo 
Closer inspection of structures 
 
4.3 AFM 
inspection 
AFM Icon-PT 
Measurement of structures
